metric registration approaches differ significantly across the three repositories:\\n\\n## Kubernetes Approach: Centralized Registry with Lazy Registration\\nKubernetes uses a sophisticated two-tier approach with `k8s.io/component-base/metrics` package. Metrics are created using `metrics.NewCounter()`, `metrics.NewHistogram()`, and `metrics.NewGaugeVec()` at the package level (pkg/controller/nodelifecycle/metrics.go:38-92). Registration occurs through `legacyregistry.MustRegister()` (staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry/registry.go:37), typically within a `sync.Once` pattern to ensure single registration. The `Register()` function (pkg/controller/nodelifecycle/metrics.go:98-107) acts as the entry point, called lazily when metrics are first needed. This pattern is consistently applied across all controllers like endpointslicemirroring (pkg/controller/endpointslicemirroring/metrics/metrics.go:137-149), nodeipam (pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/cidrset/metrics.go:81-88), and apiserver components (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/metrics.go:98-104).\\n\\n## Prometheus Approach: Dual Pattern with Auto-Registration\\nPrometheus uses both automatic and manual registration patterns. The storage/remote subsystem demonstrates auto-registration via `promauto.NewCounter()` (storage/remote/write.go:38-55), where metrics are created at package initialization and automatically registered. Conversely, the notifier subsystem (notifier/metric.go:33-108) uses manual creation with `prometheus.NewHistogramVec()` and `prometheus.NewCounterVec()`, followed by explicit registration through `r.MustRegister()` where a Registerer is passed to the constructor function `newAlertMetrics()`. The scrape subsystem (scrape/metrics.go:62-120) follows the manual pattern, creating metrics within `newScrapeMetrics(reg prometheus.Registerer)` and registering them via the provided registerer parameter. This flexibility allows Prometheus to support both global auto-registration and custom registries.\\n\\n## Grafana Approach: Global Auto-Registration\\nGrafana exclusively uses the promauto auto-registration pattern with `promauto.NewCounter()`, `promauto.NewHistogram()`, and `promauto.NewGaugeVec()` functions. Metrics are declared at package level in var blocks (pkg/services/notifications/mailer.go:24-34, pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/datasource_metrics_middleware.go:16-61). Registration happens automatically upon creation, either at package init time or module load time. This pattern is uniformly applied across all Grafana modules including datasource metrics middleware (pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/datasource_metrics_middleware.go:46-61), storage services (pkg/storage/unified/sql/rvmanager/rv_manager.go:27-56), and TSDB instrumentation (pkg/tsdb/loki/instrumentation/instrumentation.go:14-18). No explicit registration calls are needed with Grafana's approach.\\n\\n## Key Differences\\n1. **Registration Pattern**: Kubernetes uses explicit centralized registration through legacyregistry; Prometheus supports both explicit and automatic; Grafana uses automatic only.\\n2. **Registry Scope**: Kubernetes maintains a global legacy registry; Prometheus allows custom registry injection; Grafana relies on the default global registry.\\n3. **Stability Framework**: Kubernetes includes stability levels in metrics (metrics.ALPHA, metrics.STABLE); Prometheus and Grafana do not.\\n4. **Initialization Timing**: Kubernetes uses lazy registration via sync.Once; Prometheus/Grafana register at package load time.\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2928,"cache_read_input_tokens":83781,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2928},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f376515e-ff1a-473d-b2b2-576ee701b239","uuid":"89c64159-c867-404d-bebf-3942aa97b2bf"}

The `Register()` function (pkg/controller/nodelifecycle/metrics.go:98-107) acts as the entry point, called lazily when metrics are first needed. This pattern is consistently applied across all controllers like endpointslicemirroring (pkg/controller/endpointslicemirroring/metrics/metrics.go:137-149), nodeipam (pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/cidrset/metrics.go:81-88), and apiserver components (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/metrics.go:98-104).\\n\\n## Prometheus Approach: Dual Pattern with Auto-Registration\\nPrometheus uses both automatic and manual registration patterns. metric registration approaches differ significantly across the three repositories:\\n\\n## Kubernetes Approach: Centralized Registry with Lazy Registration\\nKubernetes uses a sophisticated two-tier approach with `k8s.io/component-base/metrics` package. Metrics are created using `metrics.NewCounter()`, `metrics.NewHistogram()`, and `metrics.NewGaugeVec()` at the package level (pkg/controller/nodelifecycle/metrics.go:38-92). Registration occurs through `legacyregistry.MustRegister()` (staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry/registry.go:37), typically within a `sync.Once` pattern to ensure single registration. The `Register()` function (pkg/controller/nodelifecycle/metrics.go:98-107) acts as the entry point, called lazily when metrics are first needed. This pattern is consistently applied across all controllers like endpointslicemirroring (pkg/controller/endpointslicemirroring/metrics/metrics.go:137-149), nodeipam (pkg/controller/nodeipam/ipam/cidrset/metrics.go:81-88), and apiserver components (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/metrics.go:98-104).\\n\\n## Prometheus Approach: Dual Pattern with Auto-Registration\\nPrometheus uses both automatic and manual registration patterns. The storage/remote subsystem demonstrates auto-registration via `promauto.NewCounter()` (storage/remote/write.go:38-55), where metrics are created at package initialization and automatically registered. Conversely, the notifier subsystem (notifier/metric.go:33-108) uses manual creation with `prometheus.NewHistogramVec()` and `prometheus.NewCounterVec()`, followed by explicit registration through `r.MustRegister()` where a Registerer is passed to the constructor function `newAlertMetrics()`. The scrape subsystem (scrape/metrics.go:62-120) follows the manual pattern, creating metrics within `newScrapeMetrics(reg prometheus.Registerer)` and registering them via the provided registerer parameter. This flexibility allows Prometheus to support both global auto-registration and custom registries.\\n\\n## Grafana Approach: Global Auto-Registration\\nGrafana exclusively uses the promauto auto-registration pattern with `promauto.NewCounter()`, `promauto.NewHistogram()`, and `promauto.NewGaugeVec()` functions. Metrics are declared at package level in var blocks (pkg/services/notifications/mailer.go:24-34, pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/datasource_metrics_middleware.go:16-61). Registration happens automatically upon creation, either at package init time or module load time. This pattern is uniformly applied across all Grafana modules including datasource metrics middleware (pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/datasource_metrics_middleware.go:46-61), storage services (pkg/storage/unified/sql/rvmanager/rv_manager.go:27-56), and TSDB instrumentation (pkg/tsdb/loki/instrumentation/instrumentation.go:14-18). No explicit registration calls are needed with Grafana's approach.\\n\\n## Key Differences\\n1. **Registration Pattern**: Kubernetes uses explicit centralized registration through legacyregistry; Prometheus supports both explicit and automatic; Grafana uses automatic only.\\n2. **Registry Scope**: Kubernetes maintains a global legacy registry; Prometheus allows custom registry injection; Grafana relies on the default global registry.\\n3. **Stability Framework**: Kubernetes includes stability levels in metrics (metrics.ALPHA, metrics.STABLE); Prometheus and Grafana do not.\\n4. **Initialization Timing**: Kubernetes uses lazy registration via sync.Once; Prometheus/Grafana register at package load time.\\n\"\n}\n","numLines":160,"startLine":1,"totalLines":160}}}
